सािन । देवान्नािन । हवींिष । च ॥
7. vṛithaa kṛisarasañyaavam paayasaapoopameva cha,
anupaakṛitamaansaani devaannaani haveeṇṣhi cha. vṛithaa kṛisara-sañyaavam paayasa-apoopam eva cha,
anupaakṛita-maansaani deva-annaani haveeṇṣhi cha.
मनुस्मृित प्र ेपण अध्याय ५ । Manusmṛiti Extensions Chapter 5
403
The dishes of (kṛisara) rice and sesame seeds, (sañyaavam) wheat flour and butter, 
(paayasa) milk pudding (cha)(eva) as well as (apoopam) sweet bread, (vṛithaa) made 
unnecessarily i.e. without the purpose of the yajña, (maansaani) the meat of animal 
(anupaakṛita) not sacrificed for yajña, (annaani) the foods (deva) for the divinities (cha)
and the food (haveeṇṣhi) for the offerings should be left aside as well. 5:7
The 11th – 23rd shlokas discuss the consumption of the meat of various animals. The 
consumption of meat is universally forbidden by Maharṣhi Manu.
क्रव्यादाञ्छकु
नान्सवा स्तथा ग्रामिनवािसनः ।
अिनिदर् ां
 ैकशफां
ि  ट्टभंच िववजर्येत
्
॥११॥
क्रव्यादान्। शकुनान्। सवार्न्। तथा । ग्रामिनवािसनः ॥ अिनिदर् ान्। च । एकशफान्। िट ट्टभम्। च । िववजर्येत्॥
11. kravyaadaañchhakunaansarvaanstathaa graamanivaasinaḥ,
anirdiṣhṭaañshchaikashaphaaṇṣhṭiṭṭibhañ cha vivarjayet. kravya-aadaan shakunaan sarvaan tathaa graama-nivaasinaḥ,
anirdiṣhṭaan cha ekashaphaan ṭiṭṭibham cha vivarjayet.
One (vivarjayet)should leave aside (shakunaan) the birds that (aadaan) eat (kravya) raw 
flesh e.g. the vultures, the eagles etc., (tathaa) and (sarvaan) all of the birds that 
(nivaasinaḥ) live around (graama) the human habitations e.g. the sparrows, the pigeons 
etc., (cha) as well as (ekashaphaan) the single toed animals (anirdiṣhṭaan) who have not 
been specifically declared edible e.g. the horses, the mules etc. (cha) and also (ṭiṭṭibham)
the sandpiper bird. 5:11
कलिवङ
्
कं प्लवंहं
संचक्राङ

ु
क्क
ु
टम
्
।

कसा रके॥१२॥
कलिवङ्कम्। प्लवम्। हसमं ्। चक्राङ्गम्। ग्रामकुक्कुटम्॥ सारसम्। रज्जवालम ु ्। च । दात्यहमू ्। शकसा रके
ु ॥
12. kalaviṅkam plavaṅ hansañ chakraaṅgaṅ graamakukkuṭam,
saarasaṇ rajjuvaalañ cha daatyoohañ shukasaarike. kalaviṅkam plavam hansam chakraaṅgam graama-kukkuṭam,
saarasam rajjuvaalam cha daatyooham shuka-saarike.
(kalaviṅkam) The sparrows, (plavam) the ducks, (hansam) the swans, (chakraaṅgam) the 
ruddy shelduck, (graama) the domesticated (kukkuṭam) rooster, (saarasam) the crane, 
(rajjuvaalam) the wild rooster, (daatyooham) the cuckoo bird, (shuka) the parrots (cha)
and (saarike) the mynah, are forbidden as well. 5:12

प्रतदानु ्। जालपादान्। च । कोयि नखिविष्करान्॥ िनमज्जतः । च । मत्स्यादान्। सौनम्। वल्लरमू ्। एव । च ॥
13. pratudaañjaalapaadaañshcha koyaṣhṭinakhaviṣhkiraan, 
nimajjatashcha matsyaadaan saunam valloorameva cha. pratudaan jaala-paadaan cha koyaṣhṭi-nakha-viṣhkiraan,
nimajjataḥ cha matsya-aadaan saunam vallooram eva cha. 
(pratudaan) The pecking birds, the birds with (jaala) webbed (paadaan) feet, (koyaṣhṭi)
the water crow, the birds (viṣhkiraan) that tear flesh (nakha) with their claws, the birds 
(nimajjataḥ) that dive in water (cha) and (aadaan) eat (matsya) fishes, (saunam) the 
meat from a slaughterhouse (cha) and (vallooram) the dried meal, are forbidden (eva)
as well. 5:13
बकं चैव बलाकांच काकोलंखञ्जरीटकम
्

बकम्। च । एव । बलाकाम्। च । काकोलम्। खञ्जरीटकम्॥
मत्स्यादान्। िवड्वराहान्। च । मत्स्यान्। एव । च । सवर्शः ॥
14. bakañ chaiva balaakaañ cha kaakolaṅ khañjareeṭakam, 
matsyaadaanviḍvaraahaañshcha matsyaaneva cha sarvashaḥ. bakam cha eva balaakaam cha kaakolam khañjareeṭakam,
matsya-aadaan viḍvaraahaan cha matsyaan eva cha sarvashaḥ. 
(bakam) The crane, (balaakaam) the heron, (kaakolam) the raven, (khañjareeṭakam) the 
wagtail, those animals (aadaan) that eat (matsya) fishes, (varaahaan) the pigs that feed 
(viḍ) on feces (cha) and (sarvashaḥ) all kinds (matsyaan) of fishes, are forbidden (eva) as 
well. 5:14
यो यस्य मां
सम ाित स तन्मां
साद उच्यते।

सादस्तस्मान्मत्स्यािन्ववजर्येत्॥१५॥
यः। यस्य । मां

15. yo yasya maansamashnaati sa tanmaansaada uchyate, 
matsyaadaḥ sarvamaan saadastasmaanmatsyaanvivarjayet. yaḥ yasya maansam ashnaati saḥ tat maansaadaḥ uchyate,
matsya-aadaḥ sarva-maansaadaḥ tasmaat matsyaan vivarjayet. 
(yaḥ) Who (ashnaati) eats (maansam) meat (yasya) of whatever kind, (saḥ) he/she 
(uchyate) is said to be (aadaḥ) the consumer of (tat) that kind of (maansa) meat, 
however, (aadaḥ) the consumer (matsya) of the fish is said to be (aadaḥ) the consumer 
मनुस्मृित प्र ेपण अध्याय ५ । Manusmṛiti Extensions Chapter 5
405
(sarva) of all kinds of (maansa) meats and (tasmaat) hence, one (vivarjayet)should leave 
aside the consumption of (matsyaan) the fishes. 5:15

ु । हव्यकव्ययोः ॥ राजीवान्। िसं
हतुण्डान्। च । सशल्कान्। च । एव । सवर्शः ॥
16. paaṭheenarohitaavaadyau niyuktau havyakavyayoḥ,
raajeevaansiṅhatuṇḍaañshcha sashalkaañshchaiva sarvashaḥ. paaṭheena-rohitau aadyau niyuktau havya-kavyayoḥ,
raajeevaan siṅha-tuṇḍaan cha sashalkaan cha eva sarvashaḥ.
(paaṭheena) The catfish (cha) and (rohitau) the carp fish (aadyau) should be consumed 
when given (niyuktau) for the purpose of (havya) offering in yajña or (kavyayoḥ) to the 
ancestors and (raajeevaan) the doe eyed fishes, (siṅha)(tuṇḍaan) the lion fishes (cha)
and (sarvashaḥ) all kinds of fishes (sashalkaan) with scales can be consumed (eva)
similarly. 5:16
न भ येदेकचरान ातां
  म

न। भ येत्। एकचरान्। अ ातान्। च । मगिद्वजान ृ ्॥ भ येषु। अिप । समिद्द ान ु ्। सवार्न्। पञ्चनखान्। तथा ॥
17. na bhakṣhyedekacharaanajñaataañshcha mṛigadvijaan,
bhakṣhyeṣhvapi samuddiṣhṭaansarvaanpañchanakhaanstathaa. na bhakṣhyet eka-charaan ajñaataan cha mṛigadvijaan,
bhakṣhyeṣhu api samuddiṣhṭaan sarvaan pañcha-nakhaan tathaa.
One should (na) not (bhakṣhyet) consume (mṛigadvijaan) the animals or birds (charaan)
that roam (eka) alone (cha) and those (ajñaataan) that are not known and (api) even 
those who (samuddiṣhṭaan) have been declared (bhakṣhyeṣhu) as edible but the 
qualities of their meat are unknown, (tathaa) as well as (sarvaan) all of those that have 
(pañcha) five (nakhaan) nails on each of the limbs. 5:17

 ैकतोदतः ॥१८॥
 ािवधम्। शल्यकम्। गोधाम्।खड्गकूमर्शशान्। तथा॥ भ यान्।पञ्चनखेषु। आह ः ।अनष्ट्रान ु ्। च ।एकतोदतः॥
18. shvaavidhañ shalyakaṅ godhaaṅ khaḍgakoormashashaanstathaa,
bhakṣhyaanpañchanakheṣhvaahuranuṣhṭraañshchaikatodataḥ. shvaavidham shalyakam godhaam khaḍga-koorma-shashaan tathaa,
मनुस्मृित प्र ेपण अध्याय ५ । Manusmṛiti Extensions Chapter 5
406
bhakṣhyaan pañcha-nakheṣhu aahuḥ anuṣhṭraan cha ekatodataḥ.
Out of animals with (pañcha) five (nakheṣhu) nails on each of the limbs, (shvaavidham)
the porcupine, (shalyakam) the hedgehog, (godhaam) the monitor lizard, (khaḍga) the 
rhinoceros, (koorma) the tortoise (tathaa) and (shashaan) the rabbit, (cha) and all of the
animals (ekatodataḥ) with one row of teeth (anuṣhṭraan) except the camels are (aahuḥ)
said to be (bhakṣhyaan) edible. 5:18

19. chhatraakam viḍvaraahañ cha lashunaṅ graamakukkuṭam,
palaaṇḍuṅ gṛiñjanañ chaiva matyaa jagdhvaa pated dvijaḥ. chhatraakam viḍ-varaaham cha lashunam graama-kukkuṭam,
palaaṇḍum gṛiñjanam cha eva matyaa jagdhvaa patet dvijaḥ.
By (matyaa) knowingly (jagdhvaa) consuming (chhatraakam) the mushrooms, 
(varaaham) the pigs that consume (viḍ) feces, (lashunam) the garlic, (graama) the 
domesticated (kukkuṭam) rooster, (palaaṇḍum) the onion (cha)(eva) as well as
(gṛiñjanam) the turnip, (dvijaḥ) a twice-born (patet) falls from grace. 5:19

अमत्या । एतािन ।षट्। जग्ध्वा । कृच्छ्रम्। सान्तपनम्। चरेत्॥
यितचान्द्रायणम्। वा । अिप । शेषेषु।उपवसेत्। अहः ॥
20. amatyaitaani ṣhaḍ jagdhvaa kṛichchhran saantapanañ charet,
yatichaandraayaṇam vaa’pi sheṣheṣhoopavasedahaḥ. amatyaa etaani ṣhaṭ jagdhvaa kṛichchhram saantapanam charet,
yatichaandraayaṇam vaa api sheṣheṣhu upavaset ahaḥ.
And (amatyaa) after having unknowingly (jagdhvaa) consumed (etaani) these (ṣhaṭ) six, 
one (charet) should undertake (saantapanam) the penance called (kṛichchhram)
Kṛichchhra (vaa) or (yatichaandraayaṇam) Yatichaandraayaṇa, as detailed in chapter 
eleven shlokas numbered 212 and 218, and (api) in case of the consumption of any 
(sheṣheṣhu) of the remaining inedible substances one (upavaset) should observe a fast 
(ahaḥ) for a day. 5:20

21. samvatsarasyaikamapi charetkṛichchhran dvijottamaḥ,
ajñaatabhuktashuddhyarthañ jñaatasya tu visheṣhataḥ. samvatsarasya ekam api charet kṛichchhram dvija-uttamaḥ,
ajñaata-bhukta-shuddhi-artham jñaatasya tu visheṣhataḥ.
(artham) In order to (shuddhi) cleanse from any (ajñaata) unintended (bhukta)
consumption of the inedibles, (uttamaḥ) the greatest amongst (dvija) the twice-borns 
should (api) regardless (charet) observe (kṛichchhram) the Kṛichchhra penance (ekam)
once every (samvatsarasya) year. (tu) However, (jñaatasya) for intentional 
transgressions, (visheṣhataḥ) specific penances must be undertaken. 5:21
Killing the animals and meat consumption

22. yajñaartham braahmaṇairvadhyaaḥ prashastaa mṛigapakṣhiṇaḥ,
bhṛityaanaañ chaiva vṛittyarthamagastyo hyaacharatpuraa. yajña-artham braahmaṇaiḥ vadhyaaḥ prashastaaḥ mṛiga-pakṣhiṇaḥ,
bhṛityaanaam cha eva vṛitti-artham agastyaḥ hi aacharat puraa.
(artham) For the purpose (yajña) of the yajña, (prashastaaḥ) the best (mṛiga) animals 
and (pakṣhiṇaḥ) birds (vadhyaaḥ) should be killed (braahmaṇaiḥ) by the braahmaṇa 
(cha) and (artham) for the (vṛitti) sustenance (bhṛityaanaam) of the servants (eva) as
well, as (agastyaḥ) the sage Agastya (aacharat) did (puraa) in the ancient times (hi)
indeed. 5:22

23. babhoovurhi puroḍaashaa bhakṣhyaaṇaam mṛigapakṣhiṇaam,
puraaṇeṣhvapi yajñeṣhu brahmakṣhatrasaveṣhu cha. babhoovuḥ hi puroḍaashaaḥ bhakṣhyaaṇaam mṛiga-pakṣhiṇaam,
puraaṇeṣhu api yajñeṣhu brahma-kṣhatra-saveṣhu cha.
(hi) Because (api) even (puraaṇeṣhu) in the ancient (yajñeṣhu) yajña (saveṣhu) conducted 
together (brahma) by the braahmaṇa (cha) and (kṣhatra) the kṣhatriya, 
मनुस्मृित प्र ेपण अध्याय ५ । Manusmṛiti Extensions Chapter 5
408
(bhakṣhyaaṇaam) edible (mṛiga) animals and (pakṣhiṇaam) birds (babhoovuḥ) have 
been part (puroḍaashaaḥ) of the cooked food items made for offerings. 5:23
The 26th – 44th shlokas continue the discussion on the consumption of the meat of various 
animals, which is forbidden by Maharṣhi Manu. These shlokas also provide conflicting 
information implying that these are the handiwork of different individuals.
एतदु
 ं िद्वजातीनांभ याभ यमशेषतः ।
मां
सस्यातः प्रव यािम िविधंभ णवजर्ने॥२६॥
एतत्। उ म्। िद्वजातीनाम्। भ याभ यम्। अशेषतः ॥ मां
सस्य । अतः । प्रव यािम । िविधम्। भ णवजर्ने॥
26. etaduktan dvijaateenaam bhakṣhyaabhakṣhyamasheṣhataḥ,
maansasyaataḥ pravakṣhyaami vidhim bhakṣhaṇavarjane. etat uktam dvijaateenaam bhakṣhya-abhakṣhyam asheṣhataḥ,
maansasya ataḥ pravakṣhyaami vidhim bhakṣhaṇa-varjane.
(etat) This was the list of the foods (bhakṣhya) that are fit for consumption and 
(abhakṣhyam) that are unfit for consumption (dvijaateenaam) by the twice-borns, 
(uktam) described (asheṣhataḥ) without leaving any detail out. And (ataḥ) now I 
(pravakṣhyaami)shall speak (vidhim) about the procedures (bhakṣhaṇa) of consumption
and (varjane) of avoidance (maansasya) of the meat. 5:26

ु । तु। प्राणानाम्।एव । च । अत्यये॥
27. prokṣhitam bhakṣhayenmaansam braahmaṇaanaañ cha kaamyayaa,
yathaavidhi niyuktastu praaṇaanaameva chaatyaye. prokṣhitam bhakṣhayet maansam braahmaṇaanaam cha kaamyayaa,
yathaa-vidhi niyuktaḥ tu praaṇaanaam eva cha atyaye.
(braahmaṇaanaam) The braahmaṇa should (kaamyayaa) willingly (bhakṣhayet)
consume (maansam) meat when (niyuktaḥ) appointed for performance of offerings
(yathaa) as per (vidhi) the proper procedures, (cha)(tu) and when (prokṣhitam) the meat 
has been offered on yajña, (cha)(eva) as well as when one’s (praaṇaanaam) life (atyaye)
is in danger. 5:27
प्राणस्यान्निमदंसव प्रजापितरकल्पयत
्
।
स्थावरंजङ

॥२८॥

मनुस्मृित प्र ेपण अध्याय ५ । Manusmṛiti Extensions Chapter 5

स्थावरम्। जङ्गमम्। च । एव । सवर्म्। प्राणस्य । भोजनम्॥
28. praaṇasyaannamidan sarvam prajaapatirakalpayat,
sthaavarañ jaṅgamañ chaiva sarvam praaṇasya bhojanam. praaṇasya annam idam sarvam prajaapatiḥ akalpayat,
sthaavaram jaṅgamam cha eva sarvam praaṇasya bhojanam.
(prajaapatiḥ) God (akalpayat) has created (sarvam) everything (idam) in this world 
(annam) for the sustenance (praaṇasya) of the soul and hence (sarvam) everything 
(jaṅgamam) mobile (cha)(eva) as well as (sthaavaram) immobile (bhojanam) is a food 
(praaṇasya) for the living beings. 5:28
चराणामन्नमचरा दिष्ट्रणामप्यद ं िष्ट्रणः ं ।
अहस्ता  सहस्तानांश
ू
राणांचैव भीरवः ॥२९॥
चराणाम्। अन्नम्। अचराः । दिष्ट्रणाम ं ्। अिप । अदिष्ट्रणः ं ॥
अहस्ताः । च । सहस्तानाम्। शराणाम ू ्। च । एव । भीरवः ॥
29. charaaṇaamannamacharaa daṇṣhṭriṇaamapyadaṇṣhṭriṇaḥ,
ahastaashcha sahastaanaañ shooraaṇaañ chaiva bheeravaḥ. charaaṇaam annam acharaaḥ daṇṣhṭriṇaam api adaṇṣhṭriṇaḥ,
ahastaaḥ cha sahastaanaam shooraaṇaam cha eva bheeravaḥ.
(acharaaḥ) The immobile (annam) are the food (charaaṇaam) for the mobile, 
(adaṇṣhṭriṇaḥ) those lacking teeth (daṇṣhṭriṇaam) for the ones having teeth, (ahastaaḥ)
those lacking hands (sahastaanaam) for the ones with hands, (cha)(eva) as well as
(bheeravaḥ) the docile (shooraaṇaam) for the fierce. 5:29

30. naattaa duṣhyatyadannaadyaanpraaṇino’hanyahanyapi,
dhaatraiva sṛiṣhṭaa hyaadyaashcha praaṇino’ttaara eva cha. na attaa duṣhyati adan aadyaan praaṇinaḥ ahani ahani api,
dhaatraa eva sṛiṣhṭaaḥ hi aadyaaḥ cha praaṇinaḥ attaaraḥ eva cha.
A being* (attaa) who is eligible to consume, does (na) not (duṣhyati) commit any sin 
(api) even if it (adan) eats (aadyaan) other edible (praaṇinaḥ) beings (ahani)(ahani)
everyday (hi) because (aadyaaḥ) the edible (praaṇinaḥ) beings (cha)(eva) as well as their 
(attaaraḥ) consumers (sṛiṣhṭaaḥ) are created (dhaatraa) by the sustainer (eva) only. *A 
मनुस्मृित प्र ेपण अध्याय ५ । Manusmṛiti Extensions Chapter 5
410
human is implied here and this shloka is trying to justify human indulgence in all kinds of 
meat. 5:30

सस्य । इित ।एषः।दैवः। िविधः। स्मतः॥ ृ अतः। अन्यथा । प्रवि ः। ृ तु। रा सः। िविधः।उच्यते॥
31. yajñaaya jagdhirmaansasyetyeṣha daivo vidhiḥ smṛitaḥ,
ato’nyathaa pravṛittistu raakṣhaso vidhiruchyate. yajñaaya jagdhiḥ maansasya iti eṣhaḥ daivaḥ vidhiḥ smṛitaḥ,
ataḥ anyathaa pravṛittiḥ tu raakṣhasaḥ vidhiḥ uchyate.
(jagdhiḥ) The consumption (maansasya) of meat (yajñaaya) for the purpose of yajña, 
(eṣhaḥ) this (iti) is (smṛitaḥ) considered to be (daivaḥ) the divine (vidhiḥ) procedure, 
(ataḥ)(tu) and it done (anyathaa) due to any other (pravṛittiḥ) tendencies (uchyate) is 
said to be (raakṣhasaḥ) the demonic (vidhiḥ) procedure. 5:31

32. kreetvaa svayam vaa’pyutpaadya paropakṛitameva vaa,
devaanpitṛeeñshchaarchayitvaa khaadanmaansan na duṣhyati. kreetvaa svayam vaa api utpaadya para-upakṛitam eva vaa,
devaan pitṛeen cha archayitvaa khaadan maansam na duṣhyati.
Whether (kreetvaa) purchased, (utpaadya) produced by slaughtering animals (svayam)
oneself, (vaa) or (upakṛitam) given (para) by someone else (eva) as well, if such 
(maansam) meat (khaadan) is consumed (archayitvaa) after offering it (devaan) to the 
scholars (cha) and (pitṛeen) the elders, one does (na) not (duṣhyati) incur any sins. 5:32

33. naadyaadavidhinaa maansam vidhijño’naapadi dvijaḥ,
jagadhvaa hyavidhinaa maansam pretya tairadyate’vashaḥ. na adyaat avidhinaa maansam vidhijñaḥ anaapadi dvijaḥ,
मनुस्मृित प्र ेपण अध्याय ५ । Manusmṛiti Extensions Chapter 5
411
jagadhvaa hi avidhinaa maansam pretya taiḥ adyate avashaḥ.
(dvijaḥ) A twice-born, (vidhijñaḥ) who is conversant with the procedure related to 
consuming meat (anaapadi) in non-emergency situations, should (na) not (adyaat)
consume (maansam) meat (avidhinaa) without following that procedure, (hi) because 
(jagadhvaa) after eating (maansam) the meat (avidhinaa) without following the proper 
procedure, he/she, (pretya) upon his/her death, gets (avashaḥ) uncontrollably (adyate)
eaten (taiḥ) by those animals. How would the grass grazing animals feast upon the flesh 
of these humans? 5:33

34. na taadṛisham bhavatyeno mṛigahanturdhanaarthinaḥ,
yaadṛisham bhavati pretya vṛithaamaansaani khaadataḥ. na taadṛisham bhavati enaḥ mṛiga-hantuḥ dhana-arthinaḥ,
yaadṛisham bhavati pretya vṛithaa-maansaani khaadataḥ.
Even the one (hantuḥ) who kills (mṛiga) animals (arthinaḥ) for (dhana) money, (na) does 
not (bhavati) become (taadṛisham) as laden with (enaḥ) sins (pretya) upon death, 
(yaadṛisham) as(bhavati) becomesthe one (khaadataḥ) who consumes (maansaani) the 
meats (vṛithaa) in vain i.e. without the purpose of a yajña. 5:34

35. niyuktastu yathaanyaayañ yo maansan naatti maanavaḥ,
sa pretya pashutaañ yaati sambhavaanekaviñshatim. niyuktaḥ tu yathaa-nyaayam yaḥ maansam na atti maanavaḥ,
saḥ pretya pashutaam yaati sambhavaan ekaviñshatim.
(maanavaḥ) The human, (yaḥ) who (niyuktaḥ) is appointed for the performance of the 
yajña (yathaa) as per (nyaayam) the rules, (tu) but (na) does not (atti) consume the 
offered (maansam) meat, (pretya) upon his/her death, (saḥ) he/she (yaati) goes 
(pashutaam) into the animal forms (ekaviñshatim) for next twenty one (sambhavaan)
lives. 5:35

36. asanskṛitaanpashoonmantrairnaadyaadvipraḥ kadaachana,
mantraistu sanskṛitaanadyaachchhaashvatam vidhimaasthitaḥ. asanskṛitaan pashoon mantraiḥ na adyaat vipraḥ kadaachana,
mantraiḥ tu sanskṛitaan adyaat shaashvatam vidhim aasthitaḥ.
(vipraḥ) A braahmaṇa should (na) not (kadaachana) ever (adyaat) consume (pashoon)
the animals (asanskṛitaan) that have not been sanctified (mantraiḥ) with the mantras. 
(tu) However, (aasthitaḥ)steadfast in the devotion (shaashvatam)towards the universal 
(vidhim) procedures, he/she (adyaat) should consume the ones (sanskṛitaan) that are 
sanctified (mantraiḥ) with the mantras. 5:36

37. kuryaad ghṛitapashun saṅge kuryaatpiṣhṭapashun tathaa,
na tveva tu vṛithaa hantum pashumichchhetkadaachana. kuryaat ghṛita-pashum saṅge kuryaat piṣhṭa-pashum tathaa,
na tu eva tu vṛithaa hantum pashum ichchhet kadaachana.
(saṅge) When desirous of eating meat, one (kuryaat) should make an image (pashum)
of an animal (ghṛita) using clarified butter (tathaa) and (piṣhṭa) the flour and consume 
it (tu) but should (na) not (kadaachana) ever (ichchhet) desire (hantum) to kill (pashum)
an animal (vṛithaa) in vain. 5:37

38. yaavanti pashuromaaṇi taavatkṛitvo ha maaraṇam,
vṛithaapashughnaḥ praapnoti pretya janmani janmani. yaavanti pashu-romaaṇi taavat kṛitvo ha maaraṇam,
vṛithaa-pashu-ghnaḥ praapnoti pretya janmani janmani.
(ghnaḥ) The one who kills (pashu) an animal (vṛithaa) in vain, (pretya) upon one’s death, 
(janmani)(janmani) life after life, (ha) indeed (praapnoti) gets (maaraṇam) killed (taavat)
that many (kṛitvo) times (yaavanti) as were the number (romaaṇi) of hairs on the body 
(pashu) of the animal killed by one. 5:38

39. yajñaartham pashavaḥ sṛiṣhṭaaḥ svayameva svayambhuvaa,
yajño’sya bhootyai sarvasya tasmaadyajñe vadho’vadhaḥ. yajña-artham pashavaḥ sṛiṣhṭaaḥ svayam eva svayam-bhuvaa,
yajñaḥ asya bhootyai sarvasya tasmaat yajñe vadhaḥ avadhaḥ.
(svayam)(bhuvaa) The self-created God has (svayam)(eva) himself (sṛiṣhṭaaḥ) created 
(pashavaḥ) the animals (artham) for the purpose (yajña) of the yajña and (yajñaḥ) the 
yajña is beneficial (sarvasya) for all (bhootyai) of the beings. (tasmaat) Hence, (vadhaḥ)
killing (asya) of an animal (yajñe) in the yajña (avadhaḥ) is not considered killing it. 5:39

40. oṣhadhyaḥ pashavo vṛikṣhaastiryañchaḥ pakṣhiṇastathaa,
yajñaarthan nidhanam praaptaaḥ praapnuvantyutsṛiteeḥ punaḥ. oṣhadhyaḥ pashavaḥ vṛikṣhaaḥ tiryañchaḥ pakṣhiṇaḥ tathaa,
yajña-artham nidhanam praaptaaḥ praapnuvanti utsṛiteeḥ punaḥ.
(oṣhadhyaḥ) The herbs, (pashavaḥ) the animals, (vṛikṣhaaḥ) the trees, (tiryañchaḥ) the 
animals with zigzag motion (tathaa) and (pakṣhiṇaḥ) the birds, when they (praaptaaḥ)
attain (nidhanam) death (artham) for the purpose (yajña) of the yajña, then they (punaḥ)
again (praapnuvanti) attain (utsṛiteeḥ) life in superior forms. 5:40

41. madhuparke cha yajñe cha pitṛidaivatakarmaṇi,
atraiva pashavo hinsyaa naanyatretyabraveenmanuḥ. madhu-parke cha yajñe cha pitṛi-daivata-karmaṇi,
atra eva pashavaḥ hinsyaaḥ na anyatra iti abraveet manuḥ.
(madhu)(parke) During the offerings of the honey mixture, (yajñe) in the yajña, (cha) and 
(karmaṇi) in the performances of offerings (pitṛi) for the ancestors (cha) and (daivata)
the divinities, (pashavaḥ) the animals (hinsyaaḥ) can be slain (eva) only (atra) during 
these performances and (na) not (anyatra) anywhere else; (iti) this (abraveet) was 
proclaimed (manuḥ) by Maharṣhi Manu. 5:41

42. eṣhvartheṣhu pashoonhinsanvedatattvaarthavid dvijaḥ,
aatmaanañ cha pashuñ chaiva gamayatyuttamaaṅ gatim. eṣhu artheṣhu pashoon hinsan veda-tattva-artha-vid dvijaḥ,
aatmaanam cha pashum cha eva gamayati uttamaam gatim.
(dvijaḥ) The twice-born, (vid) who understands (artha) the deeper meaning (tattva) of 
the elements (veda) of the Vedas, (hinsan) kills (pashoon) the animals only (eṣhu) in 
these (artheṣhu) contexts (cha) and (gamayati) helps (aatmaanam) oneself (cha)(eva) as 
well as (pashum) the animal attain (uttamaam) a blessed (gatim) state. 5:42

43. gṛihe guraavaraṇye vaa nivasannaatmavaandvijaḥ,
naavedavihitaaṅ hinsaamaapadyapi samaacharet. gṛihe gurau araṇye vaa nivasan aatmavaan dvijaḥ,
na aveda-vihitaam hinsaam aapadi api samaacharet.
(nivasan) While residing (gṛihe) at home, (gurau) with the guru’s (vaa) or (araṇye) in the 
forest, (aatmavaan) a sincere (dvijaḥ) twice-born should (na) not (samaacharet) engage 
(hinsaam) in any violence (aveda)(vihitaam) that is not sanctioned in the Vedas, (api)
even (aapadi) in the times of distress. 5:43
या वेदिविहता िहं

या । वेदिविहता । िहसा ं । िनयता । अिस्मन्। चराचरे॥ अिहसाम ं ्।एव । ताम्। िवद्यात्। वेदात्। धमर्ः । िह। िनबर्भौ॥
44. yaa vedavihitaa hinsaa niyataa’smiñshcharaachare,
ahinsaameva taam vidyaadvedaaddharmo hi nirbabhau. yaa veda-vihitaa hinsaa niyataa asmin chara-achare,
ahinsaam eva taam vidyaat vedaat dharmaḥ hi nirbabhau.
(asmin) In this world (yaa) whatever (hinsaa) violence (chara) against mobile and 
(achare) immobile (niyataa) is ordained (vihitaa) by the rules (veda) of the Vedas, (taam)
that (vidyaat) should be considered as (ahinsaam) non-violence (eva) only, (hi) because 
(dharmaḥ) the code of conduct (nirbabhau) originates (vedaat) from the Vedas. 5:44
मनुस्मृित प्र ेपण अध्याय ५ । Manusmṛiti Extensions Chapter 5
415
The 50th shloka advises against improper consumption of meat while Maharṣhi Manu is 
preaching against consumption of meat, altogether.
न भ यित यो मां
संिविधंिहत्वा िपशाचवत
्
।
स लोकेिप्रयतांयाित व्यािधिभ  न पीड
्
यते॥५०॥
न। भ यित । यः । मां
सम्। िविधम्। िहत्वा । िपशाचवत्॥
सः । लोके। िप्रयताम्। याित । व्यािधिभः । च । न। पीड्यते॥
50. na bhakṣhayati yo maansam vidhiṅ hitvaa pishaachavat,
sa loke priyataañ yaati vyaadhibhishcha na peeḍyate. na bhakṣhayati yaḥ maansam vidhim hitvaa pishaachavat,
saḥ loke priyataam yaati vyaadhibhiḥ cha na peeḍyate.
One (yaḥ) who (na) does not (bhakṣhayati) eat (maansam) meat, (pishaachavat) like an 
uncouth who eats (hitvaa) disregarding (vidhim) the proper procedures, (saḥ) he/she 
(yaati) becomes (priyataam) dear (loke) to the society (cha) and is (na) not (peeḍyate)
tormented (vyaadhibhiḥ) by diseases. 5:50
The 52nd – 56th shlokas present conflicting ideas implying that they were added by 
different individuals at different times. Some try to justify consumption of meat in certain 
circumstances while some others try to encourage the masses to refrain from the 
consumption of the meat by assigning great virtues to this abstinence. Staying away from 
the consumption of the meat indeed keeps one away from the related sins. However, for 
earning virtues one would have to perform some virtuous tasks.

ॄ्।देवान्। ततः। अन्यः।न। अिस्त । अपण्यक ु ृत॥्
52. svamaansam paramaansena yo vardhayitumichchhati,
anabhyarchya pitṛeendevaanstato’nyo naastyapuṇyakṛit. sva-maansam para-maansena yaḥ vardhayitum ichchhati,
anabhyarchya pitṛeen devaan tataḥ anyaḥ na asti apuṇya-kṛit.
One (yaḥ) who (ichchhati) desires (vardhayitum) to increase his/her (sva) own 
(maansam) flesh (maansena) with the meat (para) of other (anabhyarchya) without first 
offering it (pitṛeen) to the elders and (devaan) divinities, there (asti) is (na) no (anyaḥ)
other bigger (apuṇya)(kṛit) sinner (tataḥ) than him/her. 5:52
Avoidance of meat consumption
वष वष ऽ मेधेन यो यजेत शतंसमाः ।
मनुस्मृित प्र ेपण अध्याय ५ । Manusmṛiti Extensions Chapter 5

53. varṣhe varṣhe’shvamedhena yo yajeta shatan samaaḥ,
maansaani cha na khaadedyastayoḥ puṇyaphalan samam. varṣhe varṣhe ashvamedhena yaḥ yajeta shatam samaaḥ,
maansaani cha na khaadet yaḥ tayoḥ puṇya-phalam samam.
One (yaḥ) who (yajeta) performs (ashvamedhena) the Ashvamedha yajña (varṣhe) year 
after (varṣhe) year (shatam) for one hundred (samaaḥ) years (cha) and the one (yaḥ)
who (na) does not (khaadet) consume (maansaani) meat, (phalam) the fruits (tayoḥ) of 
both of these (puṇya) virtues (samam) are comparable. 5:53

54. phalamoolaashanairmedhyairmunyannaanaañ cha bhojanaiḥ,
na tatphalamavaapnoti yanmaansaparivarjanaat. phala-moola-ashanaiḥ medhyaiḥ muni-annaanaam cha bhojanaiḥ,
na tat phalam avaapnoti yat maansa-pari-varjanaat.
Even (ashanaiḥ) by consuming (medhyaiḥ) pious (phala) fruits and (moola) vegetables 
(cha) and (bhojanaiḥ) by eating only (annaanaam) the foods considered fit (muni) for 
ascetics, one does (na) not (avaapnoti) get (tat) a (phalam) reward so great (yat) as one 
gets from (pari) entirely (varjanaat) avoiding (maansa) meat. 5:54

55. maan sa bhakṣhayitaa’mutra yasya maansamihaadmyaham,
etanmaansasya maansatvam pravadanti maneeṣhiṇaḥ. maam saḥ bhakṣhayitaa amutra yasya maansam iha admi aham,
etat maansasya maansatvam pravadanti maneeṣhiṇaḥ.
(yasya) Whose (maansam) meat (aham) I (admi) consume (iha) during this life, (saḥ) it 
(bhakṣhayitaa) shall devour (maam) my flesh (amutra) in the next life, (etat) this is 
(maansatvam) the meatness (maansasya) of the meat as (maneeṣhiṇaḥ) the wise 
(pravadanti) describe. 5:55
मनुस्मृित प्र ेपण अध्याय ५ । Manusmṛiti Extensions Chapter 5

56. na maansabhakṣhaṇe doṣho na madye na cha maithune, 
pravṛittireṣhaa bhootaanaan nivṛittistu mahaaphalaa. na maansa-bhakṣhaṇe doṣhaḥ na madye na cha maithune,
pravṛittiḥ eṣhaa bhootaanaam nivṛittiḥ tu mahaa-phalaa. 
There is (doṣhaḥ) a problem (na) neither (bhakṣhaṇe) in the consumption of (maansa)
meat (cha) and (madye) liquor, (na) nor (maithune) in having sexual intercourse. (eṣhaa)
These are (pravṛittiḥ) the natural tendencies (bhootaanaam) of the beings. (tu)
However, (nivṛittiḥ) refraining from them brings (mahaa) great (phalaa) rewards. 5:56
The 58th – 104th shlokas shloka. Hence this is not considered to be written by Manu.
Causes of impurity

ू । च । सं
िस्थते॥ अशद्धाः

ू । च । तथा । उच्यते॥
58. dantajaate’nujaate cha kṛitachooḍe cha sansthite, 
ashuddhaa baandhavaaḥ sarve sootake cha tathochyate. danta-jaate anu-jaate cha kṛita-chooḍe cha sansthite,
ashuddhaaḥ baandhavaaḥ sarve sootake cha tathaa uchyate. 
(sansthite) Upon the death of a child who is either (danta)(jaate)teething (cha) or whose 
(chooḍe) head tonsuring (kṛita) has been done (anu)(jaate) before the start of teething, 
(sarve) all of his/her (baandhavaaḥ) relatives (uchyate) are considered as (ashuddhaaḥ)
impure (cha) and (tathaa) similarly (sootake) upon the birth of a child as well. 5:58
दशाहंशावमाशौचंसिपण्डेष
ु
िवधीयते।
अवार्क्सञ्चयनादस्थ्नां यहमेकाहमेव च ॥५९॥
दश । अहम्। शावम्। आशौचम्। सिपण्डेषु। िवधीयते॥
अवार्क्। सञ्चयनात्। अस्थ्नाम्। ित्रऽअहम्। एकऽअहम्। एव । च ॥
59. dashaahañ shaavamaashauchan sapiṇḍeṣhu vidheeyate, 
arvaak sañchayanaadasthnaan tryahamekaahameva cha. dasha aham shaavam aa-shaucham sapiṇḍeṣhu vidheeyate,
arvaak sañchayanaat asthnaam tri aham eka aham eva cha. 
In case of a death (sapiṇḍeṣhu) in a close relation, (aa)(shaucham) the impurity 
(shaavam) related to the dead body (vidheeyate) has been decreed to remain either 
मनुस्मृित प्र ेपण अध्याय ५ । Manusmṛiti Extensions Chapter 5
418
until (dasha) ten (aham) days, or for (tri) the three (aham) days (arvaak) before 
(sañchayanaat) the collection (asthnaam) of the ashes of the cremated, (cha) or for (eka)
one (aham) day (eva) only, depending on the intellectual level of the one who is 
grieving. 5:59

 षेस मेिविनवतर्ते। समानोदकभावस्तुजन्मनाम्नोरवेदने॥६०॥
सिपण्डता । तु।प षे
ु । स मे। िविनवतर्ते॥ समानोदकभावः । तु। जन्मनाम्नोः । अवेदने॥
60. sapiṇḍataa tu puruṣhe saptame vinivartate,
samaanodakabhaavastu janmanaamnoravedane. sapiṇḍataa tu puruṣhe saptame vinivartate,
samaana-udaka-bhaavaḥ tu janma-naamnoḥ avedane.
(sapiṇḍataa) The close relationship (vinivartate) ends (saptame) after seven (puruṣhe)
generations in the lineage (tu) and (bhaavaḥ) the feeling of inseparability (samaana) like 
(udaka) water i.e. intimacy fades when (janma) the origins and (naamnoḥ) the names 
(avedane) are not known. 5:60
यथेदंशावमाशौचंसिपण्डेष
ु
िवधीयते।
जननेऽप्येवमेव स्यािन्नप

यथा । इदम्। शावम्। आशौचम्। सिपण्डेषु। िवधीयते॥
जनने। अिप । एवम्। एव । स्यात्। िनपणमु ्। शिद्धम ु ्। इच्छताम्॥
61. yathedañ shaavamaashauchan sapiṇḍeṣhu vidheeyate,
janane’pyevameva syaannipuṇañ shuddhimichchhataam. yathaa idam shaavam aa-shaucham sapiṇḍeṣhu vidheeyate,
janane api evam eva syaat nipuṇam shuddhim ichchhataam.
(yathaa) As (idam) this (aa)(shaucham) impurity (shaavam) related to the dead body
(vidheeyate) decreed in case of death (sapiṇḍeṣhu) in a close relationship, (evam)
similarly for the ones (ichchhataam) desirous of (nipuṇam) absolute (shuddhim) purity, 
it (syaat) remains (janane) in case of births (api)(eva) as well. 5:61

62. sarveṣhaañ shaavamaashaucham maataapitrostu sootakam,
sootakam maatureva syaadupaspṛishya pitaa shuchiḥ. sarveṣhaam shaavam aa shaucham maataa-pitroḥ tu sootakam,
sootakam maatuḥ eva syaat upaspṛishya pitaa shuchiḥ.
